13:11 ACさお 画像
13:18 池田よしたか English Menu Translation
Appetizer

Fresh Cutlassfish and Garland Chrysanthemum tossed in Golden Bottarga (太刀魚と春菊の唐墨和え)

Note: "Bottarga" is used for Karasumi as it is widely recognized by foodies as a delicacy.

Sushi

Pressed Sushi of Premium "Seki Saba" Mackerel (関サバ棒寿司)

Note: Highlighted "Premium" to indicate the brand value of Seki Saba.

Soup

Clear Broth with Delicate Tiger Prawn Mousse (車海老真丈の清し仕立て)

Note: "Mousse" or "Dumpling" explains the texture of Shinjo. "Delicate" suggests the refined taste of the dashi.

Sashimi

Chef's Selection of Seasonal Sashimi - Spotted Knifejaw, Fresh Tuna, and Squid (お造り　石垣鯛　鮪　烏賊)

Note: Ishigakidai is translated as "Spotted Knifejaw," but since it is rare, you can simply call it "Premium White Fish (Ishigakidai)" if preferred.

Grilled Dish

Grilled Spanish Mackerel marinated in Miso and Citrus (鰆味噌幽庵焼き)

Note: "Yuan-yaki" implies a citrus (yuzu) marinade, so mentioning citrus adds to the appetite appeal.

Fried Dish

Lightly Fried Creamy Cod Soft Roe and Sesame Tofu in Dashi Broth (雲子と胡麻豆腐の揚げだし)

Note: "Cod Soft Roe" is the standard culinary term for Kumoko/Shirako. "Creamy" describes the texture appealingly.

Vinegared Dish

Marinated Female Snow Crab (Sekogani) with Vinaigrette (勢子蟹なます)

Meat Dish

Slow-Roasted Premium "Oita Wagyu" Beef (大分和牛のローストビーフ)

Rice & Soup

Rice cooked in a Traditional Hagama Pot Served with Red Miso Soup and Simmered Yellowtail with Daikon Radish (羽釜ご飯　赤だし　鰤大根)

Dessert

Warabi Mochi (Chilled Bracken Starch Jelly coated in Sweet Soybean Flour) (わらび餅)

💡 接客で使えるワンポイント英語
メニューを指差しながら説明する際に、以下のフレーズを一言添えると、より魅力的に伝わります。

関サバについて: "Seki Saba is a famous premium mackerel from this region (Oita). It has a great texture." （関サバはこの地域（大分）の有名な高級サバです。食感が素晴らしいですよ。）

雲子（白子）について: もし「これは何？」と聞かれたら、"It is Cod soft roe. It has a very rich and creamy taste, like foie gras." （これはタラの白子です。フォアグラのようにとても濃厚でクリーミーな味わいです。） ※海外の方は白子に馴染みがない場合が多いので、"Creamy" や "Rich" と伝えるとハードルが下がります。

羽釜ご飯について: "This rice is cooked in a traditional iron pot called Hagama. It makes the rice very fluffy and sweet." （このご飯は羽釜という伝統的な鉄釜で炊いています。とてもふっくらして甘みがあります。）
